			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-decoration:underline;">WD-40 Company Reports </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-decoration:underline;">Third</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-decoration:underline;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-decoration:underline;">Q</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-decoration:underline;">uarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-decoration:underline;"> 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-decoration:underline;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-decoration:underline;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;text-decoration:underline;"> Financial Results</font>

		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x201C;To reflect </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">the strong sales results we experienced in the third quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, we&#x2019;ve increased our revenue expectations and believe that net sales are likely to be in a range of between $4</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">75</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> million to $49</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> million for the full fiscal year</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> which reflects year-over-year sales growth of between 1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">6</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> and 2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.&nbsp;&nbsp;As things </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">get back to normal post</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">pandemic, consumer spending patterns will change</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> again</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">we expect consolidated net sales to grow </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">in the mid to high single digits</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,&#x201D; Ridge concluded.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 11pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-size:11pt;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;background-color: #FFFFFF;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;background-color: #FFFFFF;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;background-color: #FFFFFF;line-height:115%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">

The increase in sales in Latin America was primarily due to higher maintenance product sales in Mexico</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> driven by a successful&nbsp;shift to a direct distribution model&nbsp;that the company began late in the third quarter of the prior fiscal year. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">In addition, sales in Latin America in the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year were negatively impacted by disruptions and lockdowns related to the early stages of the COVID-19 pandemic</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="background-color: #FFFFFF;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
				<font style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;font-family:Symbol;background-color:#FFFFFF;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="background-color: #FFFFFF;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales in EMEA </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">increased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">80</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> quarter </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">primarily</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> due </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">to higher sales of maintenance products in both the EMEA direct and distributor markets, which increased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">85</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent and </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">70</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent, respectively.&nbsp;&nbsp;Higher sales of maintenance products in the EMEA direct markets were primarily due to increased sales of WD-40 Multi-Use Product driven by increased demand linked to renovation trends associated with the pandemic</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">increased sales through the ecommerce channel</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> and increased promotional </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">activities</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">. &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">In addition, sales in the corresponding period of the prior fiscal year were negatively impacted by disruptions and lockdowns related to the early stages of the COVID-19 pandemic. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Higher sales of maintenance products in the EMEA distributor markets were primarily attributable to improved economic conditions as a result of reductions in COVID-19 related movement restrictions.&nbsp;&nbsp;Changes in foreign currency exchange rates had a favorable impact on sales for the EMEA segment from period to period. On a constant currency basis</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> EMEA sales for the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> quarter would have increased by </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">63</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent compared to the prior fiscal year quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="background-color: #FFFFFF;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
				<font style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;font-family:Symbol;background-color:#FFFFFF;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="background-color: #FFFFFF;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:0.1pt 0pt 6pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Net sales in Asia-Pacific increased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">14</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">third</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.&nbsp; </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Changes in foreign currency exchange rates had a favorable impact on sales for the Asia-Pacific segment. </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">On a constant currency basis, Asia-Pacific would have increased by 5 percent compared to the prior year fiscal quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> primarily </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">due </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">to higher sales of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">maintenance products</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> in </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">the Asia-Pacific distributor markets and Australia which increased 26 percent and 14 percent, respectively. Higher sales of maintenance products in the Asia-Pacific distributor markets were primarily attributable to improved economic conditions as a result of reductions in COVID-19 related movement restrictions.&nbsp;&nbsp;Higher sales of maintenance products in the Australia were primarily attributable to increased sales of 3-IN-ONE and WD-40 Specialist driven by increased demand linked to renovation trends associated with the pandemic.&nbsp;&nbsp;Partially offsetting</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> these sales increases were lower sales of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">WD-40 Multi-Use Product</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> in China which decreased </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">12</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> percent </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">compared to the prior year fiscal quarter</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> primarily due to a higher level of sales in the third quarter of fiscal year 2020 associated with the timing of COVID-19 restrictions and shipping activities during that period. </font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt 0.1pt 36pt;background-color: #FFFFFF;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">As previously announced, WD-40 Company&#x2019;s board of directors declared on Tuesday, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">June 15</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 20</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> a </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">regular </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">quarterly dividend of $0.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">72 </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">per share payable on </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">July</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> 30</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;"> to stockholders of record at the close of business on </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">July </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">16</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">, 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font>

		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">About WD-40 Company</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">WD-40 Company is a global marketing organization dedicated to creating positive lasting memories by developing and selling products that solve problems in workshops, factories and homes around the world. The Company markets a wide range of maintenance products and homecare and cleaning products under the following well-known brands: WD-40&#xAE;, 3-IN-ONE&#xAE;, GT85&#xAE;, X-14&#xAE;, 2000 Flushes&#xAE;, Carpet Fresh&#xAE;, no vac&#xAE;, Spot Shot&#xAE;, 1001&#xAE;, Lava&#xAE; and Solvol&#xAE;.&nbsp; </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#x2003;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">Headquartered in San Diego, WD-40 Company recorded net sales of $408.5 million in fiscal year 2020 and its products are currently available in more than 176 countries and territories worldwide. WD-40 Company is traded on the NASDAQ Global Select market under the ticker symbol &#x201C;WDFC.&#x201D; For additional information about WD-40 Company please visit </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;text-decoration:underline;">http://www.wd40company.com</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Arial;color:#000000;">&#xFEFF;</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:0.1pt 0pt;line-height:115%;text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
